<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_cd9fbd5c-596a-4a73-927e-7b1c0fda2125'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer11327131859745681546">Twenty-seven-year-old Farrow Keene lives by his actions, and his actions say he’s the best at whatever he does. As a 24/7 bodyguard and the new boyfriend to Maximoff Hale, protecting the headstrong, alpha billionaire has never been more complicated. And one rule can’t be bent: <br/><br/><i>Keep your relationship secret from the public. </i><br/><br/>Farrow is confident he’s the best man for the job.</span>
  <span id="freeText11327131859745681546" style="display:none">Twenty-seven-year-old Farrow Keene lives by his actions, and his actions say he’s the best at whatever he does. As a 24/7 bodyguard and the new boyfriend to Maximoff Hale, protecting the headstrong, alpha billionaire has never been more complicated. And one rule can’t be bent: <br /><br /><i>Keep your relationship secret from the public. </i><br /><br />Farrow is confident he’s the best man for the job. But a twist in Maximoff’s fast-paced life sticks them with the rest of Security Force Omega and their clients. <br /><br />On the road. <br />In a sleeper tour bus. <br />For four rocky months.<br /><br />Sexual frustrations, check. Road trip drama, check. Awkward bonding, check. <br /><br />But Farrow couldn’t have accounted for a high-risk threat (identity: unknown) that targets Maximoff before the ignition even turns. And it hits Farrow — someone has it out for the guy he loves. <br /><br />Every day, Maximoff &amp; Farrow's feelings grow stronger, and together, they'll either sink or swim. <br /><br /><b>The Like Us series is a true series, one continuous timeline, that follows a family of wealthy celebrities and the people that protect them. Book 1, Damaged Like Us, should be read before reading Lovers Like Us.</b></span>

    <a title="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments"><img alt="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554228831p2/67920559.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2004617254?book_show_action=true">May 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" href="/user/show/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments">Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36326400-lovers-like-us">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2004617254" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16478643448507472483"><b> <i>“I was thinking that I want a love like theirs, the in-your-face, overjoyed kind of love that knocks you backwards—and what the fuck is stopping me?” </i></b><br/><br/><b>I'm almost 200% certain, that if one day - Krista and Becca Ritchie woke up and decided to publish their grocery list, I would hit that pre-order button and still have the same kind of anticipation. Because whether you're reading about their monthly dairy needs or the great and everlasting love between two soulmates. They will almost 200% certainl</b></span>
  <span id="freeText16478643448507472483" style="display:none"><b> <i>“I was thinking that I want a love like theirs, the in-your-face, overjoyed kind of love that knocks you backwards—and what the fuck is stopping me?” </i></b><br><br><b>I'm almost 200% certain, that if one day - Krista and Becca Ritchie woke up and decided to publish their grocery list, I would hit that pre-order button and still have the same kind of anticipation. Because whether you're reading about their monthly dairy needs or the great and everlasting love between two soulmates. They will almost 200% certainly deliver. </b><br><br><b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2004617323" rel="nofollow noopener">Like Us Series ★Character Posters</a> </b><br><br>Although, <i>Lovers Like Us </i> definitely did have its flaws, like any great piece of writing... It allowed you to overlook what was on the surface. The true success was it's robust array of characters and misfits that fit together to make the most beautiful fucking puzzle you will ever <i>feel</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“How much did he love me in our past lives?”<br>“…great, great love, it was…always you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>__________________<br><br><b>
  <u>Meet the magic</u>
</b><br><br><i>The Cobalt Empire</i> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385708._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385709._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385710._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385711._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385712._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385713._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385714._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>The Hale Geek Squad </i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385715._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385716._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385717._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385718._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>The Meadows Adventurers</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385719._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510081362i/24385720._SY540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>The Bodyguards (Security Force Omega) </i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1510081362ra/24385721.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1510081362ra/24385722.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1510081362ra/24385723.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1510081362ra/24385724.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1510081362ra/24385725.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1510081362ra/24385726.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’ve definitely seen Beckett pick up random girls at NYC nightclubs. You don’t know that he sometimes goes to private sex parties—the only reason I know is because he once told Eliot, who then let it slip to Tom. Who told Jane. Who then told me.<br>...<br>Gotta love family.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>
  <u>The magic behind the magic</u>
</b><br>A bond that is so dense, it's palpable. That is what these families alongside their bodyguards give off, it completely filled me up to the brim and I am so happy and content visiting one of my favourite story worlds. These characters have a way of sinking themselves in your heart with the little things that they do. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Akara motions his beer bottle at Donnelly. “If she asked you to push her off a cliff, what would you do?”<br>“I’d say let’s grab some parachutes first, babe.” He smirks. “Then I’d clasp her hand and we’d go down…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>There is also lots of evident character development throughout the novel, this not only makes my heart but breaks it. If you are like me, and have read the Addicted Series and everything else being part of the Fizzle Force. You are seeing these characters grow up, you are seeing your original characters grow up. If I could make time stop at the lakehouse - I fucking would. But I can't, and I don't know if I love that or hate it. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“The five?” Sana asks, hand to her heart. “I live for any photographs of them together. Can you imagine the camaraderie? The friendship? The loyalty?”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Intermission</u>
</b><br>Before I start with the next section of my review, I would like to make a couple of very important public service announcements: <br><br>- Xander Hale needs to be protected at all costs. (bitch don't fight me on this) <br>- Paul Donnelly and Luna Hale are a ship that I am whole-heartedly on board for. <br>- Thane. (that's it. take it and swallow it) <br>- I cannot. I repeat - CANNOT wait to see what Charlie's love interest is going to be. I am so ready for my world to be rocked by this snazzy Cobalt idiot, you do not even realize. <br>- I would just like a moment of silence (with nothing but the background sound of confetti popping) for this lil' moment here... <br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>“Donnelly subtly eyes them while facing us too. “Those mugs are bugging Beckett.” I can’t detect Beckett’s annoyance. But not a second later, he realigns the mugs in a neat row.<br>Maximoff gesticulates from his chest to Sulli, speaking extremely fucking empathetically to his cousin.<br>I skim him, a smile playing at my lips, and I take a swig of coffee. “He’s about to hug her.” On cue, Maximoff wraps his arms around his cousin, and she squeezes him back.<br>Akara bounces his ball. “She’ll buy a Sagittarius something for me. Wait for it…” We watch Sulli scan the shelves and then veer to a display of zodiac jewelry. She plucks a silver Sagittarius keychain off a hook.<br>Spending 24/7 with a person has this effect.”</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br><br><b>
  <u>The Plot</u>
</b><br>Okaayyyyyy, here is the iffy part for me. I did rate Damaged Like Us with 4 stars as well. Because as much as I wanted to give that and this all the stars, I couldn't get myself to. The plot was a major working point for me in this story. Some parts, it fell pretty stale and the only drive I was getting to read on was from the characters themselves. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You seriously brought Audrey’s cookies here?” I didn’t even notice him carrying them.<br>“Yeah,” Oscar says. “We didn’t know if anything would be open, Redford. I was thinking ahead.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>As much as I love Farrow and Moffy together, please don't hate me when I say that I just couldn't feel the burst of chemistry that I felt from the first novel in this one. It ran dry at some stages and although we were told there was an amazing spark between them - I couldn't actually feel it. <br>The dialogue was beautiful and desperate in it's need for the characters wants in loving each other. But sometimes, the amount of anaphora and repetition was a bit overwhelming. <br><br><b><i>"Fuck me"</i> is mentioned so many times by Moffy... At one point I sat there like "Yes, Maximoff - he is just about to fuck you. Wait another page, you impatient angel" </b><br><br><br>Other than that minor bit of plot surrounding issues that I faced, I thought it was an amazing read. I will always love these characters and I hope that anyone who picks up any KB books will love them as much too. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Virgins don’t die in horror movies,” I say and cross my arms as a breeze whips through. “You have it backwards.”<br>“Sluts die first,” Charlie says on the ground. He unbuttons another button on his white shirt. Even with the cold.<br>“Well, most of us will die then,” Oscar says, tying a bandana around his forehead.” </i>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="16478643448507472483" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2079324006?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2017-four-stars">2017-four-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2079324006" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6318472942540602997"><b>4.5 stars!!!</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510148909i/24392066._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='“description"/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Lovers Like Us</i> is the second book of ‘Marrow’ also known as Maximoff Hale and Farrow Keene. Although this couple is out to Moffy’s family and their closest friends, the world doesn’t know about their relationship. It’s not that they’re ashamed or anything like that, it’s that they both want Farrow to remain Moffy’s bodyguard and the only way he can truly protect him is if the world doesn't know. <br/><br/>Due to some vicious rumors about Moffy and Jane, Moffy and several of his cousins decide</span>
  <span id="freeText6318472942540602997" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars!!!</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510148909i/24392066._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt='“description"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Lovers Like Us</i> is the second book of ‘Marrow’ also known as Maximoff Hale and Farrow Keene. Although this couple is out to Moffy’s family and their closest friends, the world doesn’t know about their relationship. It’s not that they’re ashamed or anything like that, it’s that they both want Farrow to remain Moffy’s bodyguard and the only way he can truly protect him is if the world doesn't know. <br><br>Due to some vicious rumors about Moffy and Jane, Moffy and several of his cousins decide to go on tour and get the attention elsewhere. It’s going to be a long tour with all the bodyguards as well. On a bus. For months. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“All five of us are going on tour,” I say aloud. Letting this reality sink in. No, it’s still a-hundred-million-percent bizarre. All five of us together. Sleeping on a tour bus with our six bodyguards.. A total of eleven people on one bus. Driving across America. How’d I agree to this fucking mayhem?</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>This book was SO MUCH FUN! I seriously laughed and smiled so much! There were a lot of sweet and light moments. It wasn’t all laughs though, there are serious things going on as well. I loved that it had a little bit of everything. Moffy and Farrow are still hot as ever. I love the connection they share. Their back and forth banter is fantastic as always. I can’t get enough of this couple! <br><br>What I really loved about this book is the fact that we didn't just get Moffy and Farrow- we got a lot more of the cousins and other bodyguards as well! There are SO MANY future books I want from this gang and so many couples I ship! Krista and Becca- PLEASE keep writing these stories!!! These characters are so near and dear to my heart. Especially the HALES! #TeamHale. I love the relationships that these three (Hales, Cobalts, Meadows) have with each other, and even with the guards who are a lot like family. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>There are some moments, some small, others big, that I see and feel how much love and pride they carry for the people they protect. For three famous families. For us, and it means more to me than I can ever articulate.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> The Ritchie twins can do no wrong in my eyes. Their writing is always brilliant, and I’m completely in love with the characters they write and the stories they tell! I definitely recommend these books to all! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510148909i/24392067._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt='“description"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="6318472942540602997" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1452486959" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1452486959" />
    <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover"><img alt="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489089790p2/34338862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1452486959?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1452486959" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6443074245315201233"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509748524i/24355550._SY540_.jpg' width='450' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>NEVER have I ever loved a cast of characters as much as I love these.<br/><br/>I am going to try to review this without major spoilers and without fangirling like a fucking loon. But I make no promises (about the fan-girling part.)<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509748524i/24355551._SY540_.jpg' width='450' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book was EVERYTHING. The deepening of Maximoff and Farrow’s relationship. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I don’t have the answers,” I say seriously. “I just listen to my body.” <br/>“And what does it say?” His voice is a graveled whisper. <br/>I rake a hand through my hair. “Need. Want...You.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>The fami</span>
  <span id="freeText6443074245315201233" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509748524i/24355550._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>NEVER have I ever loved a cast of characters as much as I love these.<br><br>I am going to try to review this without major spoilers and without fangirling like a fucking loon. But I make no promises (about the fan-girling part.)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509748524i/24355551._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was EVERYTHING. The deepening of Maximoff and Farrow’s relationship. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I don’t have the answers,” I say seriously. “I just listen to my body.” <br>“And what does it say?” His voice is a graveled whisper. <br>I rake a hand through my hair. “Need. Want...You.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The family dynamics. The HYSTERCIAL moments. (I will never hear or read the word “SEPARATE” without thinking of Thatcher and cracking the hell up.)<br><br>And this gem:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“God, could you even imagine? What would I say? Hello Mr. Moretti, I’m in need of some oral assistance. Would you be so kind to spread my knees?” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br>That scene had me laughing for about 4 minutes straight.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509748524i/24355552._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love how much I laughed while reading this. If I had to sum up this book in one word, it would just be <b>FUN.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509748524i/24355553._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Each character is so distinguished (Charlie, my emotional baby I LOVE YOU. Kinney is just gold. Donnelly is the most amazing loyal hysterical muffin and I want to eat him up. Thatcher, mannnnn I can't wait to see you crack) each moment just stands out (side note - I can honestly read moments of Lo and Rose bickering and never ever EVER tire of it), and every book just makes me so much more excited for the next. (*chants* THANE THANE THANE!!!!)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509748524i/24355554._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*there’s just one TINY thing that bothered me a little in this book if I'm being completely honest. Certain words and phrases were repeated. A lot. Totally a personal pet peeve of mine but it’s something I always notice while I read. I’m sure 99% of people won’t even pick up on this. <br><br>I honestly can't wait for more books on this whole gang. NO ONE AND I MEAN NO ONE writes ensemble casts like Krista &amp; Becca and never have I read a series where the world that's been created feels SO REAL. Like I could walk around Philly and pass a Super Heroes and Scones or see one of them walking down the street. I adore every single character they've created and their books remain my most anticipated and favorite reads!<br><br>Lovers Like Us is out now! | <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2zbSKbu">http://amzn.to/2zbSKbu</a><br>Book 1: Damaged Like Us | <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2zdq7uF">http://amzn.to/2zdq7uF</a><br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467902722i/19644381._SX540_.jpg" width="275" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498677416ra/23151138.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2195986600?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=amazing-heroines">amazing-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ebooks-i-own">ebooks-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=reading-slowly">reading-slowly</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=girl-crush">girl-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=na">na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ex-hotties-in-uniform">ex-hotties-in-uniform</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2195986600" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1111818638943931201"><i>Hopefully my reading slump is over, bitches!</i><br/><br/>It’s been particularly hard for me to balance work and reading, even more when there are books I need to get through in order to read others but then there are these sort of books that make you feel free and excited and <i>light</i>. Like you could read your way through everything. <br/><br/>So thank you, LLU, for not letting me go by grabbing me and making me need to finish reading you.<br/><br/>Now, this story was such an improvement from the first book, it was a relief. I fee</span>
  <span id="freeText1111818638943931201" style="display:none"><i>Hopefully my reading slump is over, bitches!</i><br /><br />It’s been particularly hard for me to balance work and reading, even more when there are books I need to get through in order to read others but then there are these sort of books that make you feel free and excited and <i>light</i>. Like you could read your way through everything. <br /><br />So thank you, LLU, for not letting me go by grabbing me and making me need to finish reading you.<br /><br />Now, this story was such an improvement from the first book, it was a relief. I feel like my reading experiences with this series so far has been more gratifying than the material itself.<br /><br />Allow me to explain –while I enjoy reading about Moffy&amp;Farrow plus the rest of the character (whom I adore) there’s little development for the main couple. Yes, there were things they needed to sort out but they’re already <i>there</i>. They’re already a well cemented couple and don’t get me wrong, I like them, but there isn’t much for them to go forward with together.<br /><br />Unlike their issues as individuals which required a lot of time and attention. Farrow’s relationship with his father, Maximoff’s relationship with Charlie and the rest of his family, Farrow’s relationship with Lily and Lo and I could go on and on with just them. <br /><br />Add to that the bodyguards, Jane’s issues, the Hales, Cobalts and Meadows problems and dynamics that weren’t deeply or deservedly explored and you got me with a bittersweet taste after finishing this book.<br /><br />There were a lot of stuff I liked –I could read more about the bodyguards and laugh, feel and care for them, I also liked the new information we got about our characters and just read how they react to particular situations, that made my week but I’d love to see more about Jane, Sulli, MARIA, Charlie, Becket, Luna, Xander and just the rest of their siblings. I’m craving for their voices too.<br /><br />It was a highly entreating book but I need more.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1111818638943931201" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1285709479" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1285709479" />
    <a title="Corina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8905971-corina"><img alt="Corina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580618612p2/8905971.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1285709479?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Corina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Corina" href="/user/show/8905971-corina">Corina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8905971-corina?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8905971-corina?shelf=mm">mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8905971-corina?shelf=bodyguard">bodyguard</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1285709479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14189676357322249340">Lovers Like Us was absolutely FANTASTIC!!!!<br/><br/>I am a HUGE fan of Krista and Becca Ritchie.<br/><br/>One of the biggest reasons has always been that their series were unique. The Addicted Series as well as the Calloway Sisters are true series. I have NEVER read anything like this before. With each book Krista and Becca Ritchie continue a story arc that includes every single character of the cast. From the very beginning they included everyone, all the siblings, boyfriends and love interests. And whenever I re</span>
  <span id="freeText14189676357322249340" style="display:none">Lovers Like Us was absolutely FANTASTIC!!!!<br /><br />I am a HUGE fan of Krista and Becca Ritchie.<br /><br />One of the biggest reasons has always been that their series were unique. The Addicted Series as well as the Calloway Sisters are true series. I have NEVER read anything like this before. With each book Krista and Becca Ritchie continue a story arc that includes every single character of the cast. From the very beginning they included everyone, all the siblings, boyfriends and love interests. And whenever I read a book I felt like I'm part of this HUGE family, and over the years and many books I became so invested in this story and everyone's journey.<br /><br />Now diving into a new series, it took me exactly one book to fall in love with this new generation of Hales, Meadows, and Cobalts. With the first book I got a taste of what was to come, the second book I was already head over heels in love with every single character.<br /><br />Krista and Becca Ritchie managed to create a cast that was incredibly fascinating. Not only were the characters enigmatic and captivating, each individual was complex, layered and utterly unique. They also introduced a slew of bodyguards that were HOT, HOT, HOT and apparently some will be future love interests down the road. YES!!!!!!!!!! <br /><br />I fell in love with quite a few of the bodyguards. YUM!! That's all I'm saying. <br /><br />If you want to take a look at the inspirations for each characters, take a look at their Pinterest boards. EYE CANDY that's all I'm saying.<br /><br />The love story between Farrow and Maximoff was unbelievably romantic, sexy but most of all emotionally gripping. Farrow and Maximoff knew each other so well. I was sighing and swooning with each page. It's just amazing how these authors can top each book, deliver even more amazing stories, develop characters I would want to call my friends, or fall in love with myself.<br /><br />Honestly, it's incredible!!!!!<br /><br />I can't get enough of their writing, their stories or their characters. I never thought that this new generation would speak to me as deeply as they did. But I loved them all. And I can't wait to read the next book.<br /><br />I believe the reason why Lover Like Us was even better than Damaged Like Us  was because of the deep bond between Maximoff and Farrow. Those two had my heart go all gooey. I was honestly to God in LOVE!! On top of that, the authors decided to take the group (Maximoff, Jane, Sulli, Beckett and Charlie with their bodyguards) on a road trip, and the close proximity was exactly what everyone needed to fix some of the issues and grow even closer. Not only did the cousins grow closer, the entire lot, bodyguards included, became a tight knit group. For me the sense of belonging, trust and loyalty was just beautiful and heartwarming - truly one of a kind!!!<br /><br />If you want to read something UNIQUE, a series that is a bit like a reality show, give these books a try. It's an epic series that you won't easily forget. <br /><br /><br />___________________________________<br /><br /><a href="https://thebrowneyedbookworm.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more reviews and book recommendations on my blog.</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebrowneyedbookworm/" rel="nofollow noopener">Find me on Bookstagram.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14189676357322249340" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6296262079640822435"><b>4 stars for the Audiobook</b> <br/>J.F. Harding and Alexander Cendese did a good job narrating this book<br/><br/><b>2.45 stars for the story</b><br/><br/>This book is waaaaayyyyyy OTT but i still liked it. It is a soap opera that i can't stop myself from wanting to know more. And you need a family chart to get through it.<br/><br/><b>What worked</b><br/><br/>I liked, The family, i have a thing for mm books about families, they just pull me in, and here the bond between the parents, the children and the bodyguards is really satisfying to read.<br/><br/>At least there</span>
  <span id="freeText6296262079640822435" style="display:none"><b>4 stars for the Audiobook</b> <br>J.F. Harding and Alexander Cendese did a good job narrating this book<br><br><b>2.45 stars for the story</b><br><br>This book is waaaaayyyyyy OTT but i still liked it. It is a soap opera that i can't stop myself from wanting to know more. And you need a family chart to get through it.<br><br><b>What worked</b><br><br>I liked, The family, i have a thing for mm books about families, they just pull me in, and here the bond between the parents, the children and the bodyguards is really satisfying to read.<br><br>At least there was a plot in this one, a stalker of some sort, it kept me interested and i was shocked when he/she was revealed, not someone i suspected at all.<br><br>Xander need to get his story ASAP and Luna is my favorite side character.<br><br>The banter between the characters was good and i had some LOL moments.<br><br><b>What didn't work</b><br><br>I liked Farrow and Maximoff more in book 1 than in this book, it took a while to feel their chemistry, it was like they were trying too hard to prove, they are in love. Moffy is too perfect that he sometimes become boring and Farrow is so cocky that is not even cool anymore.<br><br>I still don't understand why they are famous, i kept rolling my eyes when Farrow kept saying they are protecting A-List celebrities, Like for real? What do they even do? Then i remembered the Kardashians and decided to just go with the flow or i will end up angry and it worked.<br><br>Overall it still liked it. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1530813875ra/25928764.gif" width="340" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2046578035" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8358242764602747568"><b>December 2018:</b><br/><br/>Still my least favorite of the series, but rating stands. Middle books are hard. This one especially since Moffy and Farrow have to keep their relationship a secret in public. This one doesn't have the build up of book 1 and the "HEA" of book 3. But still an enjoyable read. <br/><br/><b>March 2018:</b><br/><br/>Decided to continue on with the series and re-read book 2. Once again, just as enjoyable the second time around. It was nice because it had been awhile since I read books 1 and 2, but not gonna lie I </span>
  <span id="freeText8358242764602747568" style="display:none"><b>December 2018:</b><br /><br />Still my least favorite of the series, but rating stands. Middle books are hard. This one especially since Moffy and Farrow have to keep their relationship a secret in public. This one doesn't have the build up of book 1 and the "HEA" of book 3. But still an enjoyable read. <br /><br /><b>March 2018:</b><br /><br />Decided to continue on with the series and re-read book 2. Once again, just as enjoyable the second time around. It was nice because it had been awhile since I read books 1 and 2, but not gonna lie I kind of want to keep going and read book 3 again. That's how much I love Moffy and Farrow and this series. Rating stands.<br /><br /><b>November 2017:</b><br /><br /><b>4.5 Stars!</b><br /><br />I was a little nervous about this one. Continuing books about the same couple can be a challenge. Sometimes it's hard to top the build-up to the MCs getting together. <br /><br />In Lovers Like Us, Moffy and Farrow are a couple, albeit a secret couple. Not an aspect I was thrilled with, but I was engaged in the story wanting to see if they went public. <br /><br />Like book 1, this one was rather repetitive, especially when it came to descriptions and Moffy and Farrow constantly mooning over each other. And there was a lot going on, a lot of siblings and cousins. <br /><br />But the writing is very addictive, it sucks you in. It's choppy and not a style everyone will like. But it makes for quick reading - I was able to read 7000 locations in a day or so. <br /><br />So once again, I really ended up liking it and I'm looking forward to more.</span>

  <u>Re-read: 05.09.2018</u>
</b><br>I adore these two. Granted, this book isn't the best, but you get to see the couple get immensely closer; they get a powerful bond. And it only gets stronger. I'm practically giddy to read next one even though I've already read it.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1549554694ra/27029584.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The garden explodes with buzzing. Pinging notifications. Texts and calls.<br>People realize what’s happened, but I’m not looking. I’m not watching them.<br>We’re in our own world.<br>Our own universe.<br>No one can have it. No one can break it.<br>This moment belongs to us.</i>
  </b>

  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*The wolf scout and the bodyguard*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br>We're back with billionaire <b>Maximoff ‘Moffy’ ‘wolf scout’ Hale</b> (22) and bodyguard <b>Farrow Redford Keene</b> (27, turns 28)'s story. They are out to their family, but still have to continue keeping their relationship a secret to the outside world. Being on tour, doesn't exactly make it easier, specially not with all the sexual frustrations and the stronger, deeper connection that is forming between them. <b>Overall, the story was a tiny bit better than the first one</b>, however, I just wanted more action. I keep looking - wanting - for <i>something</i>, yet I'm not getting it. Let's hope book #3 will give it to me... Too bad we have to fucking wait for it.<br><br><b><u>Character List</u>:</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<i>Not all characters in this list will make an appearance in the book, but most will be mentioned.<br>Ages represent the age of the character at the beginning of the book. Some characters will be older when they’re introduced, depending on their birthday.</i><br><b>THE HALES</b><br><i>Lily Calloway &amp; Loren Hale</i><br>Maximoff - 22<br>Luna – 17<br>Xander – 14<br>Kinney – 12<br><br><b>THE COBALTS</b><br><i>Richard Connor Cobalt &amp; Rose Calloway</i><br>Jane - 22<br>Charlie – 19<br>Beckett – 19<br>Eliot – 18<br>Tom – 17<br>Ben – 15<br>Audrey – 12<br><br><b>THE MEADOWS</b><br><i>Ryke Meadows &amp; Daisy Calloway</i><br>Sullivan - 19<br>Winona – 13<br><br><b>THE SECURITY TEAM</b><br><i>These are the bodyguards that protect the Hales, Cobalts, and Meadows.</i><br><b>Security Force Omega</b><br>Akara Kitsuwon - 25<br>Farrow Keene – 27<br>Quinn Oliveira– 20<br>Oscar Oliveira - 30<br>Paul Donnelly – 26<br><br><b>Security Force Epsilon</b><br>Thatcher Moretti - 27<br>Banks Moretti – 27<br>Heidi Smith – 50s<br>…and more<br><br><b>Security Force Alpha</b><br>Price Kepler – 40s<br>…and more. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“She said I was moral to a fault and you can be impulsive, headstrong. We’re fucking different but we’re still two superheroes who’d die for each other. In any era, any alternate universe. Like Captain America and the Winter Solider.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (NA) Contemporary Romance (M/M)<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book Two<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes, so far. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Farrow Redford Keene.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Probably not.<br><b>Rating</b> - 3 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2050073021" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6396933475609692199">5 Lover Like Us Stars!!!<br/><br/>The ending was <b>EPIC!!!</b> I can not wait to get my hands on the next book. These boys have officially landed on my favorite couple list. <br/><br/>I enjoyed this installment more than I did <i>Damaged Like Us</i>. In this one the characters are more fleshed out. Maximoff and Farrow are in love and their relationship is deeper and more connected. <br/><br/>This one pretty much picks up where the last one left us. The rumors about Jane and Moffy are still fresh. The relationship with Moffy and Jane's pa</span>
  <span id="freeText6396933475609692199" style="display:none">5 Lover Like Us Stars!!!<br /><br />The ending was <b>EPIC!!!</b> I can not wait to get my hands on the next book. These boys have officially landed on my favorite couple list. <br /><br />I enjoyed this installment more than I did <i>Damaged Like Us</i>. In this one the characters are more fleshed out. Maximoff and Farrow are in love and their relationship is deeper and more connected. <br /><br />This one pretty much picks up where the last one left us. The rumors about Jane and Moffy are still fresh. The relationship with Moffy and Jane's parents are strained. Moffy has no idea how to fix any of it and him being him, it isn't sitting well with him. But Jane has a brilliant idea. She and her siblings have come together with an idea that will not only put these cousins in close quarters, but it just might be the answer to distracting the media and fans from these viscous rumors. The plan? Go on tour. The tour will include 5 fames: Maximoff, Jane, Charlie, Beckett, and Sullivan. They will do meet and greets, sign autographs, and do a Q&amp;A. All proceeds will go to charity. Then of course their bodyguards will be along for the ride. So that's 11 people in total on a tour bus that sleeps 12. For months. What could go wrong??? A few things here and there. A runaway sister. A stalker. A leaked video (I wish this was a visual thing dolls cause, hot damn!!!). A rivalry between cousins that escalates a few times. And lastly, a spiked bag of cookies. Through all of this we get to know this family better. We learn so much more about these bodyguards. And best of all, we get to see Morrow fall deeper in love. <br /><br />I cannot express how impressed I am with these authors and how well they have been able to insert so many characters into their books and give them each their own unique personalities. Each character has their flaws and quirks and are so well written. Like I said before, I cannot wait for the next book because boy that ending really leaves you craving for more. As in right now. LOL <br /><br />The only thing I wish I had in this book that I pray we get in the next is more intimate moments between these guys. I mean intimate tender moments. I want to see them both be a bit softer with each other and more at ease with their feelings. That's all! <br /><br />Happy reading dolls! xx</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36326400-lovers-like-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=3-stars-aint-the-devil">3-stars-aint-the-devil</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=m-m-romance">m-m-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2220519892" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1896389791706916629"><b> 3.5 stars </b><br/><br/>I always have the hardest time writing 3 star reviews. The book didn’t suck, but it also wasn’t amazing either. Let me put it this way, I started reading this book when it came out on Halloween, and only just now finished it right before Christmas. I liked it enough to finish, but not enough to read in one sitting.<br/><br/>KB Ritchie are among my favorite authors, in fact I think this is the lowest rating I have ever given their books. So while I enjoyed this book to some extent, I am also a b</span>
  <span id="freeText1896389791706916629" style="display:none"><b> 3.5 stars </b><br><br>I always have the hardest time writing 3 star reviews. The book didn’t suck, but it also wasn’t amazing either. Let me put it this way, I started reading this book when it came out on Halloween, and only just now finished it right before Christmas. I liked it enough to finish, but not enough to read in one sitting.<br><br>KB Ritchie are among my favorite authors, in fact I think this is the lowest rating I have ever given their books. So while I enjoyed this book to some extent, I am also a bit sad because usually they are 4 or 5 star authors for me.<br><br>Lovers Like Us is the second book in the Like Us trilogy, and I really loved the first book but this one dragged on a bit and was very confusing at times. I honestly couldn’t remember everyone’s names in all the extended family and bodyguards, so it was hard for me to assign a look or a personality for each character. There were so many! It felt like work and I read for pleasure, I don’t want it to be work. Opposite of that, I am in love with the Cobalt children and will continue reading this series solely for Jane’s book and for Charlie’s if they come along in the future. Charlie wormed his anti-hero self into my heart and I am dying for that man’s book!<br><br>What saved this book for me was the last 40% picked up a lot, whereas the first 60% was slow for me. Lots of banter, staring, not admitting things to each other. It didn’t click with my reading tastes. I wanted a more plot heavy story and got a more dialogue driven one.<br><br>As I said I still love the Ritchies and will read anything they read. These are two authors who I wholeheartedly believe need a lot more recognition in the romance and book world. I just won’t be jumping on Alphas Like Us like I normally would a KB Ritchie book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥<br></span>

<div id="review_1454704958" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1454704958" />
    <a title="Viv" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/45499918-viv"><img alt="Viv" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606173420p2/45499918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1454704958?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Viv" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Viv" href="/user/show/45499918-viv">Viv</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45499918-viv?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45499918-viv?shelf=2-stars">2-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1454704958" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2248140800021569196">I honestly don't know where to start, so I guess this is going to be more like a rant instead of an actual review. And if you like/love the book maybe not read this review + spoilers below so read at your own risk, here we go<br/><br/>1. I will never understand how the Like Us kids are so famous? They have famous parents sure, but you want me to believe that the whole world cares about them when they didn't do anything to earn that celebrity status, sorry can't relate.<br/><br/>2. There's a plot this time around un</span>
  <span id="freeText2248140800021569196" style="display:none">I honestly don't know where to start, so I guess this is going to be more like a rant instead of an actual review. And if you like/love the book maybe not read this review + spoilers below so read at your own risk, here we go<br /><br />1. I will never understand how the Like Us kids are so famous? They have famous parents sure, but you want me to believe that the whole world cares about them when they didn't do anything to earn that celebrity status, sorry can't relate.<br /><br />2. There's a plot this time around unlike DLU but I can't really call it a plot when nothing really happened.<br /><br />3. There's less sex this time around surprisingly but K&amp;B can't expect me to just ship them just because they talked more this book. They should've build up their relationship more in the DLU instead writing sex scene almost every chapter. Their relationship is just too rushed and even in this book I don't get why they love each other as they said they did.<br /><br />4. I'm still not a fan of Farrow. His "I can do whatever, whenever I want" attitude/mentality is just a turn off.<br /><br />5. The way K&amp;B write Moffy is just a big no. I don't get what the big deal is and why everyone love/worship Moffy so much. He's the first one everyone turns to instead of their own siblings, he's always there to save everyone. He's supposed to be selfless but the way they wrote him just make him out to be self-absorbed instead.<br /><br />6. I like some of the bodyguards but I'm really tired of the whole "we can't trust anyone outside of our family/bodyguards circle." I said it before and I'll say it again, it's not healthy. Why can't they have friends or do things outside of their little intimate circle? Not everyone in the world is out to get them. Do I have to go there with the age difference? And not to mention how more relationships from this series is going to be the kids x the bodyguards.<br /><br />7. Did we get more siblings/cousins dynamic this book? Sure, but I feel like a lot of scenes between them was there just to show what a heroic person Moffy can be.<br /><br />8. Little phrases like "sharpen jaw," "sharp as ice" or "fuck me" need to go. A phrase is good once or twice but when you overuse it, it just lose it's meaning.<br /><br />From the plot to the characters, this book was too over the top for me, I just can't buy any of it. <br /><br />Personally I feel like they should've just ended the series with SKOP or give each kid a stand-alone (instead of making people read a continuous series like this) or not make the kids famous. I want to read about the kids falling in love, struggling to find their passion, going to college, dealing with famous parents, etc, but not this. I'm tired of the whole famous people vs. media plot line. We did that for ten whole books with the Addicted Series. Wasn't that enough? Everything here feels like a cheap recycling of the old books.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2248140800021569196" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2047522468" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2047522468" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2047522468?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2047522468" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16553671598377824434">4 ★'s <br/><br/>At the end of Moffy and Farrow's first book <i>(Damaged Like Us)</i>, it had just came out that they were dating and everyone had to have their noses stuck in their business...some a little too much. <br/><br/>Moffy and Farrow learn to deal but it's tough. They want to be able to kiss and touch each other when they want but they are keeping their relationship secret from the public and Farrow is still Moffy's bodyguard. <br/><br/><u>
  <b>Hands down</b>
</u> this is the best sexual chemistry EVER! Holy Hell!! And I'm not talking </span>
  <span id="freeText16553671598377824434" style="display:none">4 ★'s <br><br>At the end of Moffy and Farrow's first book <i>(Damaged Like Us)</i>, it had just came out that they were dating and everyone had to have their noses stuck in their business...some a little too much. <br><br>Moffy and Farrow learn to deal but it's tough. They want to be able to kiss and touch each other when they want but they are keeping their relationship secret from the public and Farrow is still Moffy's bodyguard. <br><br><u>
  <b>Hands down</b>
</u> this is the best sexual chemistry EVER! Holy Hell!! And I'm not talking about the steamy scenes! It's so obviously how much these two love each other that I don't know how people didn't figure it out. It is sooo intense! And to be honest, at first I thought it was a bit over the top but then I came to want that and I could care less about all the other stuff going on. <br><br>The book starts off a bit in the past with a fight between Moffy and Charlie. It's not good and their relationship just deteriorates from there. I wish we would've gotten more about Charlie since he really follows his own beat and is hard to figure out. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509726595ra/24353447.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The eldest five cousins decide to go on a meet and greet tour for their charity across country...in ONE bus...with ALL their bodyguards. Things are a little cramped to say the least...and a little confusing to say a lot. I mean, they are all wealthy...couldn't they fly? And as far as the tour goes, I understand why it was set up but most of them hate being in the public like that...seems like there could have been a better way. <br><br>But...<i>but</i> The Hot Santas might have been the best idea ever. I know I would have loved to see that. And I did like getting to know the bodyguards a little better although sometimes it was a little hard to keep all the details separate. <br><br>We also have "someone" who's out to get Moffy. It makes Farrow's job even crazier and he walks a fine line between bodyguard and boyfriend. Even more crazier was who it turned out to be as I had a totally different person picked out, well, until about the seventy-five percent mark and that died a horrible death...thank goodness. <br><br>So, there's a lot of drama as always. The cousins were great. I love Moffy and Janie! But what I really liked was the seemingly path some of the cousins and some of the bodyguards were taking AND I'm totally on board! The more, the merrier! ;) <br><br>But can we talk about that ending? OMG....I LOVED IT SOOOO MUCH! Moffy and Farrow...<b>Lovers Like Us</b> indeed. I cannot wait for the next book, <i>Alphas Like Us</i> (sooo fitting), but there's no release date at this time.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16553671598377824434" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1572815281" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1572815281" />
    <a title="Andrea" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10105567-andrea"><img alt="Andrea" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605932169p2/10105567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1572815281?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andrea" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andrea" href="/user/show/10105567-andrea">Andrea</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781682309872" href="/book/show/37003396-lovers-like-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10105567-andrea?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10105567-andrea?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10105567-andrea?shelf=favorite-characters">favorite-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10105567-andrea?shelf=road-trip">road-trip</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10105567-andrea?shelf=lgbtqiap">lgbtqiap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10105567-andrea?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1572815281" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5258174936928854012">This was so much better than Damaged Like Us. Everything that I did not like in book 1 was fixed here, and for that <b>I. Am so. Happy.</b><br/><br/>While reading Damaged Like Us I never really understood how Farrow was different from every other person Moffy had slept with besides the fact that he was his bodyguard. I am so happy that this book gave us the opportunity to see their relationship deepen. I was so excited to see other parts of their relationship – like their insecurities and fears – besides the sex</span>
  <span id="freeText5258174936928854012" style="display:none">This was so much better than Damaged Like Us. Everything that I did not like in book 1 was fixed here, and for that <b>I. Am so. Happy.</b><br /><br />While reading Damaged Like Us I never really understood how Farrow was different from every other person Moffy had slept with besides the fact that he was his bodyguard. I am so happy that this book gave us the opportunity to see their relationship deepen. I was so excited to see other parts of their relationship – like their insecurities and fears – besides the sexual aspect of it. Honestly Moffy and Farrow were cute af here, and I could cry just thinking about them.<br /><br />The family dynamics. Bitch, I’m dead. This was also missing in DLU, but I could forgive it because I know it’s the first in a series. But now it’s Book 2, and I am so happy that we got to see so much from Moffy’s family. We got to see so much from characters we didn’t see in DLU, and I was ecstatic. I always love how KB write their friendships and family dynamics. I loved seeing both the great and not so great relationships between everyone. The bodyguards as well brought most of the humor into the book and thanks to Farrow’s POV we got to learn a lot more about them. And I swear to god if Donnelly doesn’t get a book one day I will revolt.<br /><br />I love that this story didn’t just focus on Moffy and Farrow. We got so many glimpses into the lives of their loved ones and it makes me soooo excited for the future of this series. I know book 3 is also in Moffy and Farrow’s POV (which I’m fine with), but I am so ready for Janie and Sulli to shine in their POVs.<br /><br />Charlie. Charlie, Charlie, Charlie. I love him <i>so</i> much. The one thing that kind of annoyed me was how everyone kept saying how perfect Moffy was (and I know it’s not true or his fault that they say that.) So I’m really glad Charlie got a lot of pages time to kind of act like the voice of reason when it came to this.<br /><br />My biggest peeve of DLU was how Moffy and Janie’s parents reacted to the rumors at the end of the book. I know a lot of people think that how they reacted was normal under the circumstances… I’m just not one of them. So I’m glad that they apologized and are taking strides to make it up to them. Also, I was worried the rumor at the end of DLU would play a bigger part here, and I’m relieved it actually didn’t.<br /><br />Also, tiny annoyance: what’s with so many “forest-green” eye references? Like why can’t you just say “green”, or why do you even have to say the color? Why not just say “my eyes”? We get it. His eyes are forest-green, enough. The same thing was done in DLU too.<br /><br />But anyway I digress, I thought this was so much more “classic KB” book that the first which makes me really happy (did I say that already?). This got me so pumped for the series in general and I cannot wait for book 3!<br />----</span>
  <a data-text-id="5258174936928854012" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1560396564" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1560396564" />
    <a title="Ailin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25551518-ailin"><img alt="Ailin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555017708p2/25551518.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1560396564?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ailin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ailin" href="/user/show/25551518-ailin">Ailin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36326400-lovers-like-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25551518-ailin?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25551518-ailin?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25551518-ailin?shelf=the-ones-i-didn-t-like">the-ones-i-didn-t-like</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25551518-ailin?shelf=amazing-covers">amazing-covers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1560396564" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17556985445115890990">So I usually make detailed reviews with developed points and reasons for when I have too many thoughts about a book, but I honestly, truly feel like this book doesn't deserve my time and effort placed in such a long review, so this will be a bit simpler than usual.<br/><br/>With my <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1548402725?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>review for the previous book</a> I tried not to be so harsh and more open at believing it could improve, even if it was just a little bit, especially because something similar happened to me when I started Addicted Series. However,</span>
  <span id="freeText17556985445115890990" style="display:none">So I usually make detailed reviews with developed points and reasons for when I have too many thoughts about a book, but I honestly, truly feel like this book doesn't deserve my time and effort placed in such a long review, so this will be a bit simpler than usual.<br /><br />With my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1548402725?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">review for the previous book</a> I tried not to be so harsh and more open at believing it could improve, even if it was just a little bit, especially because something similar happened to me when I started Addicted Series. However, since the same unbearable nonsense kept going, I've just decided to stop sugar-coating stuff and be straight up honest about it, cutting to the chase.<br /><br />My thoughts made simple:<br />* Both our self-absorbed, arrogant protagonists are <b>still</b> incredibly unbearable and <b>still</b> lack any emotional connection, which makes it really hard not to skip all their oversexualized scenes.<br />* The books in this series seem to be led by the strong sense of "telling but not <i>showing</i>", i.e.: maximoff's "pure" and "good" and "selfless" (???) reputation, Farrow's "better than anyone" attitude, their emotional connection, as I've already stated, and many more.<br />* The "plot" of this book (if it could even be called that) is ridiculous??? Not to mention this "representation" of bodyguard tropes and "famous people" which is so far-fetched I couldn't stop rolling my eyes at it.<br />* Charlie and Eliot are the only thing that could remotely save this book.<br />* If you by any chance think this bodyguard+client relationship failed, don't worry, you'll have more than three <i>other</i> chances of reading a trope like this later on in the series, because most of these kids are apparently set to end up with bodyguards, since the rest of the world is crap and can't be trusted. Please note the sarcasm in this affirmation.<br /><br />I really don't want to engage into analyzing and criticizing this even more bc it could take me forever, and it would just be wasted time, but honestly if you want to read a good book about a bodyguard trope, go read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30176334-royally-endowed?ac=1&amp;from_search=true" rel="nofollow noopener">Royally Endowed</a> by Emma Chase, which actually makes sense and deals with the bodyguard definition in a more realistic way. Plus you'll find an actual connection between the protagonists and an actual plot. Everything this book lacks.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17556985445115890990" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16133699428319847815">Me for the next week... month... year...<br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509491332ra/24327237.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yep, definitely through the new year. Because ain’t no book hangover like a Hale/Meadows/Cobalt/Krista and Becca Ritchie book hangover. <br/><br/>I do this to myself every damn time. I know it’s going to be great and I know I’m going to be devastated when I read the last page yet I still pull an all-nighter and fly through these books. But I wouldn’t have it any other way because Krista and Becca are my favorites. Lily and Lo are my favorites and now Maximoff and F</span>
  <span id="freeText16133699428319847815" style="display:none">Me for the next week... month... year...<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509491332ra/24327237.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yep, definitely through the new year. Because ain’t no book hangover like a Hale/Meadows/Cobalt/Krista and Becca Ritchie book hangover. <br><br>I do this to myself every damn time. I know it’s going to be great and I know I’m going to be devastated when I read the last page yet I still pull an all-nighter and fly through these books. But I wouldn’t have it any other way because Krista and Becca are my favorites. Lily and Lo are my favorites and now Maximoff and Farrow are my favorites. Wait, Connor Cobalt is my absolute favorite. Rose, Ryke, Xander, the entire SFO: my favorites. Hell, they are all my favorites! <br><br>I wish the Hale/Meadows/Cobalt world was real. It certainly feels real every time I hit refesh at midnight on release day and promptly pull an all-nighter. If you’re keeping track, that’s 12 all-nighters spent with these characters. And I love them all. Not one character feels less than 100% authentic. Even the new guys, the SFO bodyguards, are making me feel like part of the family. Like I personally know these people and what they are going through. (I’m not a crackpot.) <br><br>For 12 all-nighters, I have laughed, and cried, and swooned, and smiled ridiculously for hours on end while reading and living these amazing characters. So I also have to say this every damn time too because I can’t help myself and I need these books: Keep writing, Krista and Becca. Please never stop.</span>
