<span id="freeTextContainer3942769302872117370"><b>4.5 stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509588528i/24339363._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='430' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>WOW. I loved this book so freaking much that I feel like I cannot even process how much that love is. <br/><br/>When I read Damaged Like Us I was so eager to read it that I read it in one sitting. But with this book, I loved it so much that I kept stopping myself from reading more. Because I didn't want it to end. <br/><br/>I love that with this book we get to see so much more of not only Farrow and Moffy but the rest of the gang. It's no secret that I love all the characters (especially secondary and sec</span>
  <span id="freeText3942769302872117370" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509588528i/24339363._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="430" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WOW. I loved this book so freaking much that I feel like I cannot even process how much that love is. <br><br>When I read Damaged Like Us I was so eager to read it that I read it in one sitting. But with this book, I loved it so much that I kept stopping myself from reading more. Because I didn't want it to end. <br><br>I love that with this book we get to see so much more of not only Farrow and Moffy but the rest of the gang. It's no secret that I love all the characters (especially secondary and security) and this book gave me all I wanted and MORE.<br><br>But what I loved most about this book was Moffy and Farrow. I loved that we got to see more of them together, their relationship developing and growing. They are so cute together, every time they talked I was grinning so hard I felt like a cartoon character with heart eyes all the damn time. But they are so cute and I love how they love each other. <br><br>I love Jane so much and this book only solidified my love for her. But I also loved how we got to see more of her family. Beckett surprised me but I'm so ready to see more of him. Charlie made me actually sympathize with him when previously I was feeling kind of annoyed with him. But wow, after this book I understand him so much more and I really, really like his character. <br><br>Sullivan is the sweetest girl I loved every scene we got with her. I love that we get hints of her and what she's going through but not enough to say it takes over the story (same for Jane and the rest of the gang). We get just enough to keep up curious and satisfied and I truly cannot wait to read her book it's going to be a favorite I can already tell &lt;3 <br><br>And of course I cannot write this review without mentioning my favorite security force Omega. I love them so much! Truly, the friendships that they have with one enough is so amazing and one of the best parts of this series. Thatcher is my absolute favorite but really, I love every single one of them. Donnelly makes me laugh so freaking hard, Quinn is so sweet, Akara is so badass, honestly I just love them and would love a book for all of them.<br><br>I want to go on and on but I honestly cannot say more without spoiling. The plot was so engaging and I couldn't stop thinking about this book the moment I started. So, so good! I think I love this one more than the first and I'm dying for the third book already! </span>

Krista &amp; Becca are phenomenal writers and have created such an amazing world with their series. What stands out the most are the diverse group of characters. In the Addicted series the amount of characters weren't as high as the Like Us series. And you know what.. I LOVE IT! I love every damn character and their unique thinking and personalities. Damaged Like Us didn't end with a cliffhanger, which I appreciated. In this book the gang needs to do some major damage control and lower the media attention on their families. Maximoff, Jane, Sulli, Beckett, Charlie and their six bodyguards are going on tour. I really loved the setting of this book and the super fun time they had. The bodyguards are HILARIOUS! In this book we get to know them a little better. I don't read a lot of MM romances, but I am kind of addicted to it because of DLU and LLU. And oh man, things got even better in this one. I mean there were a lot of conflicts with the paps and media and even Charlie but when it came to Marrow, it was perfect.   <b>His forest-greens flit to the Philadelphia Eagles hoodie I’m wearing. Shit, I love being his first. Even for the simple, little things. He’s been basically eye-fucking me for the past hour, but more sensual than a rough, quick fuck. If eyes could make love, his eyes would be making love to me.</b>
</i><br /><br /><i>
  <b>“You know what I was thinking while my parents recited their vows today?” Farrow shifts his weight like he’s bracing for impact. “What?” “I was thinking that I want a love like theirs, the in-your-face, overjoyed kind of love that knocks you backwards—and what the fuck is stopping me?” I pause. “And I realized the answer is me.” Farrow takes a tight breath. “What are you saying?” “I’ve been fucking stubborn, but I’d rather be stubborn with you than without you.” I’m more assured than I’ve ever been. “I’m not standing in my own way anymore. I think if you read this without reading the Addicted/Calloway Sisters series you will feel lost. So to get a better understanding of everything going on with these characters you would be better off reading their parents' series beforehand, and guys it's so damn worth it! <div id="review_2171939584" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2171939584" />
    <a title="River " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34852389-river"><img alt="River " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487674730p2/34852389.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2171939584?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="River " class="user" itemprop="url" name="River " href="/user/show/34852389-river">River </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36326400-lovers-like-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34852389-river?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2171939584" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16375486923362448162">it''s no secret that I love krista and becca, They are in my top 3 authors, so yes I'm biased sometimes but I have to be honest, I was a bit more nervous about this book than the previous one. <br/>I love the first one but I'm aware that without having background it can be a lot, because there are so many characters that we fans know and love plus a lot of bodyguards, so my question was, would they solidify these characters or would they get lost in the crowd?<br/><br/>I am happy (and a bit disappointed in mys</span>
  <span id="freeText16375486923362448162" style="display:none">it''s no secret that I love krista and becca, They are in my top 3 authors, so yes I'm biased sometimes but I have to be honest, I was a bit more nervous about this book than the previous one. <br />I love the first one but I'm aware that without having background it can be a lot, because there are so many characters that we fans know and love plus a lot of bodyguards, so my question was, would they solidify these characters or would they get lost in the crowd?<br /><br />I am happy (and a bit disappointed in myself for doubting) to say that it was AMAZING. we didn't only get to fall more in love with the 5 older kids (and luna, because let's be honest she's the best) but we really got to know and fall hard for the bodyguards. I need at least 15 more books. Everyone needs a story. <br /><br /><br />Maximoff and Farrow: <br />There was relationship development which is awesome, I thought it might be hard because they were on a road trip with 9 other people but they found the time and honestly their love warms my heart. One of the things I deeply love and respect of Krista and Becca's writing is the fact that they don't really create OTT relationship drama. Their characters deal with a lot of stuff but you always know that the couple is solid. <br />I'm really nervous for what's the come, the way things ended definitely left the characters in an interesting situation and we'll see how they deal with it. <br /><br /><br />Jane and Tatcher:<br />Nothing really happened here but the seeds for this romance were definitely planted in this book and I just can't wait to get their story! <br /><br /><br />Sulli/Akara/Jack: <br />Again, nothing really happened between these people but the non-existent triangle was resolved at least for us readers, we know now what each of these men are going to mean for Sulli going forward. <br /><br />Beckett and Charlie: <br />My favorite twins! (after KB of course) I love them! There weren't many interactions between them but the few that we saw made us see that they are inseparable and they protect each other fiercely. It was really nice to get to know them more, we got some insight into both of their lives.<br /><br />The bodyguards:<br />For a book with such a big cast it seems unrealistic to really get attached to every character but it was done so good here, it is impossible not to like these men. Every one of them is amazing.<br />Special shout-out to Donnelly, love if my life. <br /><br /><br />Luna:<br />The most amazing/important/out of this world character in the series. This girl is everything and needs to be protected. Don't have anything else to say. <br /><br />The parents:<br />I liked how those conversations/issues were handled, I really did. It was nice seeing everyone make amends and Lily ships Marrow now so I'm ready for more of that in the next book. <br /><br /><br />There was a bit of mystery and kuddos to the writing because I really didn't see that one coming. It was soooo good! <br />I like the path the series is taking and I'm really looking forward to more books.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16375486923362448162" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I love how the issues that were left hanging from Damaged Like Us and from the beginning of Lovers Like Us were resolved by the end of the book. I love the depth of each character that <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7056935.Krista_Ritchie' title='Krista Ritchie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Krista Ritchie</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2754148.Becca_Ritchie' title='Becca Ritchie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Becca Ritchie</a> creates; they seem like "real" people and it's what mak</span>
  <span id="freeText1895636931987062098" style="display:none">I was so engrossed in this book that I didn't realize when I turned the last page that I had reached the end of the story.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509898168ra/24368790.gif" width="400" alt="nooo" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I hate it when that happens. <br><br>So, I love how this book starts right where we left off in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21427834.Damaged_Like_Us__Like_Us___1_" title="Damaged Like Us (Like Us, #1) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Damaged Like Us</a>. I love how the issues that were left hanging from Damaged Like Us and from the beginning of Lovers Like Us were resolved by the end of the book. I love the depth of each character that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7056935.Krista_Ritchie" title="Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Krista Ritchie</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2754148.Becca_Ritchie" title="Becca Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Becca Ritchie</a> creates; they seem like "real" people and it's what makes them so relatable and what makes me want more. Krista and Becca are seriously the only authors I know who give us that "more." Each character's traits and personality, the way they speak, the way they act, and every little thing that makes them who they are...I can't help but wonder how in the world these authors keep track and not get confused. Krista and Becca are wonder twins for sure. <br><br>Their writing is phenomenal. I'm not only interested in the main characters but the side characters as well. I loved getting more of Jane and Moffy's siblings. And Sulli too! I loved getting to know more about the bodyguards. I loved the friendship and family bonds. I just love so much about this book! <div id="review_1807081029" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1807081029" />
    <a title="Liber_Lady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/61302386-liber-lady"><img alt="Liber_Lady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508890494p2/61302386.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1807081029?book_show_action=true">Nov 01, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Liber_Lady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Liber_Lady" href="/user/show/61302386-liber-lady">Liber_Lady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36326400-lovers-like-us">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1807081029" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5387571889996455405">5+++ STARS<br/><br/>Tell me your experience of this book if you haven't read the Addicted series and known the Hales, Cobalts and the Meadows for twenty years.<br/><br/>The Like Us series is so much special for all the fans that have loved the Hales, Cobalts and Meadows since years. We have seen them in their early 20s and throughout their 10 books, we have seen them in their early 40s.<br/><br/>The Like Us series begins with Maximoff Hale (The Eldest Hale Son, who we have known for almost 4 books in the Addicted series). An</span>
  <span id="freeText5387571889996455405" style="display:none">5+++ STARS<br /><br />Tell me your experience of this book if you haven't read the Addicted series and known the Hales, Cobalts and the Meadows for twenty years.<br /><br />The Like Us series is so much special for all the fans that have loved the Hales, Cobalts and Meadows since years. We have seen them in their early 20s and throughout their 10 books, we have seen them in their early 40s.<br /><br />The Like Us series begins with Maximoff Hale (The Eldest Hale Son, who we have known for almost 4 books in the Addicted series). And seeing him fall in love with someone makes it extra special for me.<br /><br />It is a known fact among the KB Ritchie fans that their first book of any series is a "Setting up the Plot". <b> THE MAIN FUN BEGINS WITH THE SECOND BOOK </b> <br /><br />Lovers like Us was such an AWESOME BOOK. It was by far the funniest book of the entire series. We see the love between Moffy and Farrow grow, and we see them facing different/never-ending obstacles in their life. After the debacle of the last book, the eldest kids decide to go on a ROAD TRIP...<br /><br />YES.<br /><br /><b>A ROAD TRIP IN A BUS. 5 COUSINS. 6 BODYGUARDS. </b><br /><br />There were funny moments, emotional moments, tense moments, moments where you combusted, and some Oh-so-Naughty moments. <br /><br />One of the best things about these authors is the way they capture the little moments. Their books are made of the everyday life and the little things that makes us want to be in their world with the favorite characters. Their writing puts so much of life in their characters, that you start knowing them, understanding them even when they don't explain it to you. Every book of this author is almost 400-500 pages long, and <b>YOU ALWAYS WANT MORE..!!</b> It is their beautiful writing that keeps you hooked to this world and never come out of it. Every character is so relatable that you cannot but enjoy these books to fullest. <br /><br />So if you haven't read this series, then GO AHEAD PICK IT UP..<br /><br />And if you truly want to experience the beauty of what I know is <b> THE BEST ROMANCE SERIES IN THE HISTORY, PICK IT UP FROM ADDICTED TO YOU, AND STICK WITH THESE CHARACTERS FOR THE TEN BOOKS. <br /><br />YOUR LIFE WILL NEVER BE THE SAME.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="5387571889996455405" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1909287781" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1909287781" />
    <a title="Ari " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39598773-ari"><img alt="Ari " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577904181p2/39598773.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1909287781?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ari " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ari " href="/user/show/39598773-ari">Ari </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1909287781" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8969898615887970888"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I've been fucking stubborn, but I'd rather be stubborn with you than without you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <i>*3.5 Stars!*</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Damaged Like Us</i> is my most disappointing read for 2017 so I went into <i>Lovers Like Us</i> with no expectations so I wouldn't have to deal with being disappointed again. I'm happy to say that I did enjoy this sequel a bit more than the first book, but the series itself still has some flaws.<br/><br/><i>Lovers Like Us</i> picks up some time after the rumors about Moffy and Jane being in a romantic relationship</span>
  <span id="freeText8969898615887970888" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I've been fucking stubborn, but I'd rather be stubborn with you than without you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b>
  <i>*3.5 Stars!*</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>Damaged Like Us</i> is my most disappointing read for 2017 so I went into <i>Lovers Like Us</i> with no expectations so I wouldn't have to deal with being disappointed again. I'm happy to say that I did enjoy this sequel a bit more than the first book, but the series itself still has some flaws.<br /><br /><i>Lovers Like Us</i> picks up some time after the rumors about Moffy and Jane being in a romantic relationship have died down and things are slowly getting back to normal. There is still a bit of tension now that Moffy and Farrow have come out to their family and the security team about being in a relationship so in hopes of turning all this negative attention into something positive, the group decides to go on tour to meet their fans and help raise money for a good cause. But that's easier said than done.<br /><br />I wasn't too excited to read yet another book about Moffy and Farrow and I'm really glad that this sequel didn't focus so much on this relationship. Instead we got to see more of the secondary characters and the security team. Jane is my favorite and I'm patiently waiting for her book. I feel like she deserves so much more than she gets and I just want her to be happy. The security team is a fucking riot! I couldn't not keep a straight face while reading their scenes and I'm looking forward to getting to know all the guys better as the series continues.<br /><br />I'm just going to come right out and say it: I don't think I will ever like Maximoff Hale. I'm so tired of his "god-like" complex and the fact that everyone goes to him when they're in trouble. I don't get the obsession at all and I think Charlie Cobalt expressed all my thoughts about Moffy perfectly. Farrow is okay, I guess? I just feel that because Farrow's world revolves around Moffy, we don't really know who he is without Moffy at his side and I kind of want to get to know that Farrow. I'm very curious to see how things turn out for these two in the final installment because things are definitely about to get crazy now that the cat is out of the bag but I'm going to probably keep my expectations low once again so I don't hype myself up too much.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8969898615887970888" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink?shelf=drama-llama">drama-llama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink?shelf=hate-to-love">hate-to-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink?shelf=sweet-guy">sweet-guy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink?shelf=guys-in-security">guys-in-security</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2172073299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16273498007883058208">I read this book a while ago and never got around to reviewing it.<br/><br/>I'll also be quick because right now I barely have the time to breathe in my life. So, this book... I definitely liked it more than the first. The stars should still be 4.5 because I loved it but I'm not raving about it and now raving is a requirement for the 5 stars.<br/><br/>Anyway, I adore Farrow and Maximoff. They are such an unconventional couple. Teasing each other, bantering and challenging each other is in integral fun part of their</span>
  <span id="freeText16273498007883058208" style="display:none">I read this book a while ago and never got around to reviewing it.<br /><br />I'll also be quick because right now I barely have the time to breathe in my life. So, this book... I definitely liked it more than the first. The stars should still be 4.5 because I loved it but I'm not raving about it and now raving is a requirement for the 5 stars.<br /><br />Anyway, I adore Farrow and Maximoff. They are such an unconventional couple. Teasing each other, bantering and challenging each other is in integral fun part of their relationship which I totally appreciate.<br /><br />Also, the plot was very original. The tour, the added stranger danger, their romance which is not so hidden anymore. The way it all evolved felt natural and swoony.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"She said I was moral to a fault and you can be impulsive, headstrong. We're fucking different but we're still two superheroes who'd die for each other. In any era, any alternate universe. Like Captain America and the Winter Soldier.</b>
</i><br /><br />Jane was not as present and honestly, I liked it that way. I'm sooo curious about her and Thatcher, but until that book, I'm glad that here Moffy and Farrow were front and center.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>I've slept in the same bed with him enough to know that he's typically bot a cuddler until a couple hours into sleep. It's a private, personal fact that tabloids would crave and reprint a hundred times. And it's all mine for safekeeping.</b>
</i><br /><br />We also have tons of funny moments, like the hot Santa contest or the night in the pub between the guys. I appreciate authors who can manage many characters at the same time. And the Hales, Meadows, Cobalts and bodyguards are like one huge quirky family.<br /><br />Kudos also for the mystery added to this instalment which had be scratching my head and then bashed upside the nape because I'd been cashing on someone else all along.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Oscar fastens his gaze on me, not able to restrain a smile. "It's almost growing on me. You two... together." He bites into his bagel. "Though I didn't realize you like them young, Redford --"<br />"You don't realize a lot of things, Oliveira," I cut him off, "still, we try not to hold it against you."</b>
</i><br /><br />As for style, as previously stated in my first review, the authors truly know how to craft unique characters and stories. Being bored was not an option.<br /><br />I would definitely recommend it and I'm sure I'll keep reading books in this series.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"I love you," he says deeply. "And when you hurt, I hurt."<br /><br />****<br /><br /><i><b>"I was thinking that I want a love like theirs, the in-your-face, overjoyed kind of love that knocks you backwards -- and what the fuck is stopping me?" I pause. "And I realized the answer is me."</b></i></b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16273498007883058208" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7lgb6aipT/vKttCEtITamTDEcNuam6BpeVwjInUfU/5qW/TBCT987zFnuEmTAIXijZLmUSVw7Vd08qXp+liQ7A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nRHTLy8yUtxPk6wrQEt/4vHLgrq1y9XR4GE0kwDLDLYZEjwHjqRhyLRCxOZnzyCZTJ0UMAogmO/tz7JYj4zPpA==')})
  }
